therof caplm ii thou shalte vnderstōde holy chirche two maner lyues saynt gregory sayth whyche cristen men shold sauf one called actyf greg ye contēplatyff wythout one thise ii noo man may sauid actyff lyf lieth loue charyte shewed outwarde gode bodely werkes fulfillyng goddis cōmaūdementes vii werkes mercy bodely ghostly man̄es euyn cristen lyf longeth worldly men whiche haue richesse plenty worldly goodes spende soo whiche haue state offyce cure men haue goodes spende lerid lewde temporell spirytuell generally worldly men boūde fulfylle myght cūnyng reson discrecōn asketh moche good haue moche gode doo lityll haue lesse may doo yf nouȝt haue then̄e must haue gode thise ben werkes actyf lyf bodely ghostly also grete part actyf lyf lyeth grete bodely dedes whiche man dooth bē actiff helpe right moche ordeneth man begī nyng come cōtēplatyf lyf yf thei bē vsed descreciō ¶of contēplatiff lyf werkes therof caplm iii contēplatyf lyf lieth perfyte loue charite felyd traueyle body spirite come lyf nygh thou mayst suche meanes thou hopest best neuertheles telle meanes shall tell fyrst lityll lyf contēplatyff thou myȝt somwhat see sithen set marke sighte thy soule wherto thou shalt drawe thyn occupacōn ¶of fyrst part contēplacōn caplm iiii· contemplatyff lyf hath thre partes fyrst lyeth knowyng god ghostly thynges geten reason techyng man studye holy wrytte wythout ghostly affeccōn iuly sauour felyd specyall yefte holy ghost parte haue specyally lettred men grete clerkes whiche longe studye trauaylle holy wrytte comen knowyng lesse subtilte kyndly witt contēplacōn hath ghostly sauour god ne inwardly swetnes whiche noo man maye fele yf grete charyte proper welle lorde whyche cometh none alien maner knowyng comyn gode badde maye wythout charyte dispose hem doo ¶why men shold worship low hēself owne herte vnd al caplm xviii then̄e seest thou somwhat thou shalt nother deme men ne conceyue ayenst hem wylfully none euyll suspicōn thou shalt nedefull thise shold plese god descrecōn bodily werkes ca xxii iii thyng whiche nedeful haue thy begyn̄yng hole stable entēcōn saey hole wyll desire on̄ly plese god charyte without whiche al nought ¶how men shold pray wheron poynt thought shall sette prayer caplm xxv bvt desirest thou perauenture knowe thou sholdest praye vpon thyng thou shold sette poynt thy thought thy prayer also prayer best maye charyte therfore nedeth moche adradde meke haue thus sayth iames thapostle deus superbis resistit· hūilibus autē dat graciā lorde sayth ayenstondeth proude men meke men yeueth grace whiche grace propirly charyte mesure thy mekenes shal thou haue charyte thou haue mekenes inperfitly oonly wyll affeccōn thenne shall thou haue inperfyte charyte good suffyseth saluacyon dauyd sayth inperfectū meum viderūt oculus tui lorde wyth thyn eyen mercy thou seest myn inperfeccyon yf thou haue mekenes perfytlyp then̄e shalt thou haue perfyte charyte best tother behouyth v nedely haue yf wyll saaf shold desire thenne yf thou aske perfytely meke thou shalt noo haue mekenes tyme meke sothfastly knowith hymself ¶how mā shal wyte moche wrath enuye hyd grounde herte caplm lxix tourne yet ayen ymage yf thou wolt assay moche yre enuye hidde thyn herte thou felyst loke well beholde thyself wysely whan suche stirynges yre enuye ayenst thyn euen crysten spryngen oute thyn herte styred thou arte malencoly bytter wycked wyll ayenst hym ymage thou grutchest inpacyence eyther ayēste god ony trybulacōn syknes bodily disese sente god ayenst thyn euen cristen oughte dooth ayenst lesse ymage ihesu refourmed saye suche grutchynges flesshly angrynes dedely synnes saye letten clennes herte pee conscyence thou maye haue full charyte ye whiche thou sholdest come lyf contemplatyf ende purpoos sayeng thou sholdest oonly clense thyn herte fro dedely synnes also fro venyall moche thou myghtest groūde synne myghte grace ihesu cryst somwhat slecket ¶by token thou shalt know yf thou louest thyn enmye ensample thou shalt take cryst loue hym caplm lxx though soo thou felyst none euyll ayenst thyn euen crystē tyme yet arte thou syker grounde yre quenched ne yet arte thou lorde vertue charyte suffre hym towche lityll angry shrewde worde thou shalt fele anone yf thyne hert yet made hole fulnes charyte thou arte styred euyll willed ayenst persone· ferder arte thou fro charyte yf thou nought styred ayenst persone neyther angry chere outwarde· ne noo preuy hate thy herte dispyse deme hym set hym noughte shame vylanye dooth worde dede pyte cōpassion thou hast hym thou woldest haue man mynde thinkyth yu canst fynde thyn herte hate hym loue soo gode hymself praye hym helpe hym desiryng amendyng oonly wyth thy mouth ypocrytes doo wyth affeccōn loue thyn herte then̄e haast yu perfite charite thyn euen crysten charyte saynt stephen perfitly whan prayed hem stoned dede charite coūseyled cryst wold perfite folowers whan said thus diligite inimicos vrōs vn̄facite hiis qui oderūt vos c·m v • loueth enmyes doo good hem haten prayeth hem pursuen therfore yf thou wol folowe cryst lyke hym crafte lere loue thyn enmyes synfull men thise arn thy euen crystē loke bethynke cryst yet though done thise sayd soth ouermore whan iudas toke hym kyssed hym called hym frende charyte shewed cryst vnto iudas whyche knewe dampnable noo maner feynyng ne flateryng sothfastnes good loue clene charyte though soth iudas worthy haue ony yefte god ony sygne loue wyckidnes neuertheles worthy skylfull lorde shold sheew loue goodnes creature dide iudas saye loued hym synne ne loued hym chosen loued saynt peter loued hym asmoche creature shewed hym token loue yf wolde haue amended therby folowe sōwhat yf thou maye though thou art stoken hous wyth thy body· neuertheles thyn herte folow criste loue charyte loue euen crysten eche man good bad frendes fooes wythouten feynynge flaterynge dispisyng herte ayenst man angrynes malicyous repreuyng sothly begyleth hymselfe nerer weneth ferder cryste sayd hem wolde hys discyples thꝰ hoc est preceptū meū vt diligatis inuicem sicut dilexi vos biddyng ye sholde loue togyder haue loued yf ye loue haue loued then̄e ye discyples sayste thou shalte thou loue hym badde aswell hym good vnto thys saye thus thou shalt loue bothe good badde charite cause shall telle thou shalte loue thyn euen cristen thyself yu shalt loue thyself on̄ ly god elles god god thou louest thyself whan yu arte ryghtfull grace vertuous louest thyself oonly ryghtwysnesse vertues god yeuyth ye thenne louest thou thyself god thou louest thyselfe god also god thou louest thyself yf thou dedeli synne woldest made ryghtfull wertuous then̄e louest thou thyself thou arte thou arte vnryghtful thou woldest ryght soo shall thou loue thyn euen crysten ben good rightfull thou shalt loue hem charyte god oonly ben good ryghtful thenne louest thou god hem goodnes ryghtwysnes yf ben badde dedely syn̄e thyn enmyes haten whiche thou hast full euydēce grace yet shalt thou loue hem arne ne good men ryghtfull men arn badde vnryghtfull thou shalt loue hem god myghte good ryghtful soo shalt thou noo thynge hate hem thynge contrary ryghtwysnesse synne vndstonde techyng saynt austyn departe loue man fro hate synne loue thyn euen crysten meke wolde sothfastly loue thus euen crysten· none ¶how man shall knowe moche couetyse hidde herte caplm lxxi· lifte well vppe ymage loke well abowte thou shalt mowe see couetyse loue erthly thynges occupye grete partye ymage though seme lityl thou hast forsaken rychesse moche hauour worlde art spered dongeon hast thou forsaken clenly loue hope yet lesse maystry forsake worldly good forsake loue perauē ture thou hast forsaken thy couetyse thou hast chaunged fro grete thynges smale fro pownde vnto peny fro siluer pece vnto disshe halfpeny symple chaunge thou arte noo good marchaunt thyse ensamples arn chyldisshe neuertheles betoken thou trowe assaye thyself thou haue loue delite hauyng holdyng ony thyng thou hast suche wyth ye whiche loue thou fedest thyn herte tyme yf thou haue desire yernyng haue som̄ thyng yu haste wyth whyche desire thyn herte traueyled stourbled vnskylfull belynesse clene desire vertu god maye rest therin token couetise ymage yf thou wolte assaye better loke yf ony thyng thou hast taken awaye fro maystry borowyng ony wise thou maye gete ayen thy thou arte disesed angred trowbled thyn herte bothe thou wantest thyng thou woldest haue maye haue also ayenste hym hath yu arte styred stryue chyde wyth hym myghte restore ayen wyll token thou louest worldly goodes thus done worldly men whan good rychesse takē fro hem arn heuy sory angry chidynge striuyng ayenst hem haue openly worde dede thou doost thyn hert pryuely god seeth yet thou art defawte worldly man yu hast forsaken lyckenes loue worldly thynges worldly man hath therfore exscused though stryue pursue goodes lawfull wayes haue hem ayen sayest thou behoueth haue thy necessaryes suche thynges longen well worldly man graunte well therto thou sholde loue self ne likyng haue holdyng ne ye kepyng ne sorowe ne heuynesse fele lesyng ye withdrawyng saynt gregory sayth asmoche sorow thou hast lesyng thinggreg▪ moche loue haddest thou kepyng therfore yf thyn herte made hoole thou haddest sothfastly felt desire ghostly thynges wyth syghte leest ghostly thynge ye loue likyng ony erthly thynge thou sholdest sette noughte sholde cleue vpon loue haue nedeth skylfully oonly luste likynge grete defawte also fetchen thi loue vpon ye thinge nedeth selfe defawte soo grete haue vsen thyng nedeth wythoutē loue kynde nede asketh wythoutē whiche thyng maye vsed noo defawte • othli poynte trowe many haue state lyknesse pouertee arn moche letted hyndered fro loue god ne accuse noo man ne noo state reproue eche astate arn good arn one thyng saye euery man woman hath taken state wylfull pouerte whether religyous seculer degree longe loue affeccyon bounden fastened glewed wyth ye loue ony erthly thing hath wolde haue may haue ne fele sothfastly clene loue clere syghte ghostly thynges augꝰ saynt austyn sayd lorde thus lorde loueth lytill ye louyth ony thynge wyth loueth ye loue couetyse ony erthly thynge wyth lesse loue god thyn herte though loue erthly thyng putteth hem oute charite yf soo moche strangle loue god euen crysten sothely hyndreth hem letteth hem fro feruour charyte also fro speciall mede whiche shold haue blisse heuen perfite pouerte grete losse yf myghte see soo myght know ghostly mede good precyous worthy aye lastynge wolde loue erthly ioye hauour erthly thyng yf myghte haue wythoutē syn̄e lette ne lesse lest mede blysse heuē whiche myghte haue yf wold speke ferther doo praye doo thus saye ye grace god thou maye ony man soo wyll comforte herte yf maye haue saye myghte haue ony creature whiche hath receyued plente grace see thenne syth couetyse naked grounde letteth man woman soo moche fro ghostly felyng loue god moche then̄e letteth combreth worldly men wym̄en whiche wyttes bodily besynes nyghte daye studye traueyle myghte gete ryches plente worldly good none delyte haue worldly thinges ne wyll seche say hem tyme wrytyng speke hem saye yf myghte see wolde see doo sholde doo soo ¶how man shall knowe whan synneth etynge drynkyng whan synneth venyally whan dedely caplm lxxii yet maye thou see ymage though derke flesshli loue thiself glotenye accidie lecherye thise flesshly likynges maken man full bestly ferre fro inly sauour loue god fro ye clere syghte ghostly thynges sayest thou syth behoueth nedelynges ete drynke slepe may thou doo wythouten likyng therfore thynkyth lykynge noo synne vnto saye yf thou kepe etynge drynkynge nedefull thynges thy body mesure thy nede thou receyuest noo likynge kynde askyth alle thou doost ghostely delite whiche thou felyst thy soule graūte ye forsothe thou thenne synnest ryght nought therin thenne thou well ete slepe sothly wythouten doubte full ferre fro knowyng ferd fro werchynge ete haue kynde cūne ete maye grace god saynt poul grace cunnyng sayth hymself thꝰ vbi que oībus institutus sū scio saciari esurire habū dare penuriā pati phil iiii oīa possū eo qui cōfortat enformed kenned thynges hūger ete wyth plente wyth pouerte maye hym strenghthith saynt austyn sayd tyll lorde thus lorde thou hast teched sholde take mete medicine augꝰ hūger syknes kynde mete medicyne ther therfore likyng comyth wyth asmoche kyndly nedfull noo syn̄e whan passith lust wylfull likyng then̄e synne therfore ther̄ lyeth maystrye cūne departe wysely nede fro luste wylfull likyng soo knytte togyder one comyth wyth harde receyue one nede repreue wylfull luste whiche ofte comyth vnd colour nede neuerthelesse syth soo yt nede groūde this▪ nede noo synne man neuer soo holy hym behouyth ete drynke slepe therfore luste likynge comyth vnd colour nede passyth nede lesse syn̄e man synneth dedely comynly glotenye yf encombred wyth dedely synnes beforn done then̄e may lyght lyer synne dedely soth chesyth luste lykynge flesshe delytes welfare mete drynke full reste herte wolde neuer haue lyffe ne blysse lyue euer suche lust flesshe yf myght dowte y• syn̄eth dedely loueth flesshe god lyeth dedely synne pryde enuye suche soo blynded bi deuill y• tyme hath power free wyll therfore may well ayenstōde flesshly likynges whan come falleth wylfully hem best dooth karyon asmoche hath generall wyll god principally cause dedely syn̄e therfore ye lust glotenye whiche falleth lyghtly hym dedely synne makith none ayēstondyng generall ne specyall nother man woman whiche grace charite hath alway good generall wyll god soule wheder slepe wake ete drynke good dede yt dooth soo euyll whiche wylle desire chesyth god aboue thyng hath leuer forbere thyng worlde wrathe god loue wyll though generall soo grete vertue bi grace lorde ihū yf falle freelte lust likyng mete drynke suche siknes either excesse tomoche etyng often gredely lustly delicatly tosone vntyme saueth hym kepith hym fro dedely syn̄e soth aslonge charite dedes kepyth generall wyll dooth namly yf knowe amō ge owne wretchidnes crye mercy purpose specyally ayēstonde suche fleshly lustes lord good mercyfull thise venyall syn̄es glotenye foryeuyth ryght sone vnto meke soule stiryng likyng glotenye asmoche hardest flee bi cause nede ye bodily kynde amōge syn̄es moost exscuable leest perillous therfore thou shalt ryse ayenst groūde syn̄e yu shalt ayenst syn̄es ye grounde synne oonly nede whiche maye escaped yf thou wylt doo worse slee ye nede many foles done whyche sholden slee theyf spare true man saye sholden slee vnskylfull luste wilfull likyng spare kepe bodily kynde thei doo soo ayēst syn̄es thou shalt aryse destroye oonly dedely synnes grete venyals also ayenst grounde hem moche thou mayst see skylle thou maye lyue wythout mete drynke thou may lyue wythout lecherye yf thou wyll neuer better therfore thou shalt flee on̄ly dede whiche dedely synne also wylfull likyng thyne herte withouten dede whiche venyall syn̄e somtyme dely also thou shalt traueyle ayenst groūde destroye felyng risyng flesshly stiryng ¶how groūde lecherie shold destroyed ghostli traueyle wyth bodily caplm lxxiii bvt clennes ghostly felyng god arn full heuy paynfull bitter moche eschewe spiryte maye fele kyndly sauour wt tyll flesshe haue loste bestly sauour wythouten ¶that hūger bodily paynes letteth moche goostly werchynge caplm lxxv· therfore yf thou wolt come clennes herte behouyth ayenstonde vnskylfull stiryng flesshly desyres ayenst grounde thou shalt ryse haue sayde grounde nede kyndely hūger whiche thou shal nedelynges fele tent therto tyme helpe thyself ayenst medicyne mete thou woldest helpe thiself resonable ayenst bodily syknes thou myght freely serue god bothe bodily ghostly wyte doo • thou skylfully longeth kepe thy bodily kynde vpon reison suffre god thenne sende wyll hele syknesse take gladly grutche ayēst god wylfully thou saye take thy mete commyth ordeyne yf nede vppon derknes ymage synne comyth wyndowes therof caplm lxxviii lifte vp thy lanterne see ymage fyue wyndowes whiche synne comyth thy soule ye prophete sayth 〈1 paragraph〉 mors ingreditur per fenestra wyndowes wyttes caplm lxxxi bvt sayest thou thou doost soo thou seest noo worldly thinges ne herest none ne hast none vse thy bodily wyttes nede asketh thy thou art enclosed saye thou thus hope thou doost thenne hast thou stopped grete wyndow ymage yet arte thou syker thou hast stopped priue hole ymaginyng thyne herte yf thou see wyth thy bodily eye thou maye see thy soule ymagynacōn soo mayst forberyng good saye shall paynful hym dedely synne venyall sholde ben ne saye knoweth dedely fro venyall fleeth ¶whan vse wyttes ben dedely syn̄e whan venyall caplm lxxxii neuertheles dele shall saye paynfull derknes lust wretchyd lyfe exyled flemyd oute fro herytage heuen sholde haue yf stonde stylle ye wretchydnes erthe afterwarde prison helle haue wythoute ende fro whyche pryson ye heuenly herytage myghte neuer haue come agayen yf refourmed fyrste shappe fyrste lickenes refourmynge myghte made none erthly man euery man myscheyff none myghte suffyse helpe hymselfe soo moche lesse nother man therfore nedeth done hym man oonly god skylfull sholde refourme restore man blysse yf sholde saaf whiche endles goodnes fyrste shope hym therto thenne myghte refourmed refourmed fyrste lyckenes hym fourmed grace god shall telle entente wrytynge ¶how neded mankynde oonly thorugh passyon cryste sholde restored refourmed forshape fyrste synne caplm ii ryghtwysnes god asketh trespace done foryeuen yf amendes made yf maye done sooth mankynde hole adam fyrste man trespassed ayenste god soo wonder greuously whan forfeyted speciall byddyng hym assented false counseylle fende deserued ryghtfully haue departed fro hym dampned helle wyth outen ende soo ferforth stondynge ryghtwysnesse god myghte foryeuen yf amendes first made full satysfaccyon therfore amendes myghte noo man make man oonly comen oute adam kyndely generacyon skylle trespasse vnworshyppe endles grete therfore passyd mannys myghte make amendes also skylle hath trespassed shall make amendes hym behouyth yeue hym hath trespassed vnto owyth though trespassed also ouer hym behouyth yeue sōwhat owyth oonly trespassed mankynde wherewyth myghte paye god trespaas ouer oughte hym good dede man myght doo body soule dette euery man oughte gospel sayth loue god wyth herte al soule myghtes better myght doo neuertheles dede suffyced refourmynge mankynde ne myghte doo yf fyrst refourmed thenne neded yf mannes soule sholde refourmed trespaas made good lorde god hymselfe sholde refourme ymage make amendes trespaas sythen noo man myghte myghte doo godhede myghte ne oughte make amendes sufferynge payne owne kynde therfore neded sholde take mankynde trespassed become man myghte doo comyn lawe generacion impossyble goddis sone borne towchyd woman therfor̄ hym muste become man thorugh gracyous generacyon werkynge holy ghoste clene gracyous mayden lady saynt mary soo done lorde ihesu goddis sone became man thorugh precyous deth suffred made amendes fader heuen mannys gylte myghte well doo god oughte hymselfe moche man borne kynde adam firste trespaced soo though oughte owne persone hymself myghte synne neuerthelesse oughte free wyll trespaas mankynde whiche mankynde toke saluacyon man endeles mercy soth neuer man myghte yelde god ony thynge owne oughte oonly thys blessyd ihesu myghte paye god one thyng oughte hymselfe nought one thynge yeue precyous lyfe wylfull takynge dethe loue sothfastnes oughte moche good myghte doo worshyp god lyfe dette take dethe loue ryghtwysnesse bounde therto bounde ryghtwysnesse bounde deye dethe oonly payne ordeyned man owne synne lorde ihesu synned neuer ne myghte synne therfore oughte deye thenne sythen oughte deye yet wilfully deyed thenne payd god oughte sythen beste mannes dede moost worthy euer done therfor̄ resonable synne mankynde sholde foryeuen moche man kynde founde man kynde wythoute wem̄e synne ihesu myght make amendes trespaas done myghte paye lorde god oughte ouer oughte thenne syth lorde ihesu god man deyed thus saluacyon mannes soule ryghtfull synne sholde foryeuen mā ne soule ymage sholde mow reformed restored fyrste lyckenesse blysse heuen passion lorde precyous dethe grounde refourmynge mannes soule wythoute whiche myght neuer mannes soule haue refourmed lyckenesse hym ne come blysse heuen blessyd maye werkynge soo thorugh vertue precyous passion brennyng swerde cherubyn droue adam oute paradyce put awaye endles gate heuen arn open euery man wylle entre therto persone ihesu bothe god kynge heuen blysse fader man porter yate redy receyue euery soule wyll refourmed lyf lyckenesse maye euery soule yf wyll refourmed lyckenesse god syth trespaas foryeuen amendes thorugh ihesu made fyrste gilte neuertheles though sothe soules haue profyte ne frute precyous passyon ne ame refourmed lickenes ¶that iewes paynems also false crysten men ben refourmed effectuelly thorugh vertue passyon owe defawte caplm iii two manere men arne refourmed vertue passyon one hem trowe hem loue iewes paynems haue benefyce passyon trowe iewes trow ihū sone virgyn mary goddis sone heuen also paynems trowe souereyne wisdom god wold become sone man mā hede wolde suffre paynes deth therfore iewes helde prechynge crosse passyon cryste noughte sclaunder blasphemye paynems helde noughte fantome folye true crysten men helde souereyne wysdom god grete myghte thus sayd saynt poul predicamus vobis cristū crucifirum iudeis quidem scandalū gentibus autem stulticiam ip̄is autē vocatis iudeis grecis xp̄m dei virtutem et dei sapienciam preche ye trowe ihesu cryst crucyfyed sone mary goddis sone souereyne vertue wysdom god whiche ihesu iewes paynems trowe hym sclaunder foly therfore thise men vntrouthe putten hemselfe fro refourmynge owne soule stondynge vntrouthe shall neuer saaf ne come blysse heuen sothe fro begynnyng worlde vnto laste endynge neuer man saaf ne shall saaf yf trouth generall specyall ihesu cryste come come righte chosen soules incarnacōn vnder olde testamente hadden trouthe cryste sholde come refourme mannes soule eyther openly patryarkes prophetes holy men hadde elles pryuely generally chyldern symple inperfyte soules hadden knewe specyally pryuyte incarnacyon ryght soo chosen soules vnder newe testamente hathe trouthe cryste come eyther openly felyngly ghostly men wyse men haue elles generally chyldern haue deyen crystned symple lewde soules haue arne nourysshed bosom holy chyrche syth sothe thenne thynketh thyse men gretly greuously erren sayen iewes sarrasyns kepynge owne lawe maye made saaf though trowen ihesu cryste holy chyrche trowyth moche wene owne trouth good syker suffysaunt saluacyon trouthe done semyth many good dedes ryghtwysnesse perauenture yf knewe crysten fayth better owne wolde leue owne take therfore sholde saaf naye ynough soo cryste god man bothe waye ende medyatour betwyx god man wythoute hym maye noo soule reconsyled ne come blysse heuen therfore trowen hym god man maye neuer saaf ne come blysse men also louen cryste passion arne refourmed soule lycknesse hym thise men arne fals crysten men whiche arne oute charytee lyuen deyen dedely synne thyse men trowen well semyth ihesu goddis sone passyon suffysyth saluacōn mannes soule trowe also artycles fayth vnshaply trouthe dede loue hym ne chese frute passyon lyen stylle synne false loue worlde vnto laste ende soo ben refourmed lyckenesse god goon paynes helle endelesly iewes blysse ¶of two maner refourmynges ymage one fulnesse nother fayth caplm iiii sayest thou may soth ymage god whiche man̄es soule might refourmed lyfe lyckenesse ony creature semyth naye myghte soo yf refourmed thenne sholde haue stable mynde clere syghte clere brennynge loue god ghostly thinges euerlastyngly beginnynge noo creature thou trowest liuynge lyfe ayenst thyself thou canst wel saye ghostlines neither pryue myȝtes thi soule wc ne bodyly felynge wythoute wherfore ye thynken myghte ymage myghte refourmed elles yf myght refourmed then̄e askest thou myght refourmed answere saye thus cōmaundementes god cunnynge whan soo wycked stirynges euyll wylles rysen hertes pryde enuye yre lecherye ony hede synne ayenstonde hem stryuen ayenst hem dysplesynge wyll soo folowe dede thyse wycked wylles neuerthelesse yf falle lyghtly ayenste wyll thorugh freelte vncūnynge soone conscyence greuyth hem pynyth hem soo greuously mow haue noo reste tyll shryuen maye haue foryeuenes sothly thise soules thus lyuen refourmynge ben founde therin houre dethe shall saaf come full refourmynge blysse heuen though soo myghte neuer haue ghostly felynge ne inwarde sauour ne specyall grace deuocōn lyfe tyme elles yf thou say noo soule shall saaf refourmed ghostly felynge myght fele deuocōn ghostly sauour god soules doon thorugh specyall grace then̄e sholde fewe soules saaf rewarde multytude nay trowe soules oonly arn deuoute bi grace come ghostly felyng noo moo lorde ihesu sholde haue take mankynde suffred harde passyon dethe lityll purchaas hym haue come fro ferre soo nere fro soo hye soo lowe soo fewe soules nay mercy spradde larger soo neuertheles contrary wyse yf thou trowe passyon lorde soo precyous mercy somoche shal noo soule dampned namely noo crysten man doo neuer soo euyll fooles wene soothly thou erreste gretely therfore goo meane holde middes trow holy chirche trowyth moost sinfull man lyueth erthe yf torne thorugh grace fro dedely synne wyth sothfaste repentaunce seruyse god refourmed soule yf deyed state shall saaf thus behighte lorde prophete sayenge thus quacū que hora conuersus fuerit peccator ingemuerite· xxviii vita viuet et non morietur tyme synful man
